# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-102">Устаревшие члены в .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-103">В этой статье перечислены члены типов, устаревшие в .NET Framework 4.5 и выше.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-104">Члены типа группируются по сборкам.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-105">В этой статье не перечисляются члены устаревших типов.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-106">См. [список устаревших типов](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-1108">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-1108">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-1109">Сборки IEHost.dll и IEExec.exe удалены из .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-1109">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-1110">Все их типы и члены устарели и не поддерживаются, начиная с .NET Framework 4.5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-1110">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in .NET Framework 4.5 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-1111">Эти сборки использовались для размещения элементов управления Windows Forms и для запуска исполняемых файлов в Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-1111">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4dbd4-1112">Взамен этой технологии рекомендуется использовать ClickOnce, XAML-приложения браузера (XBAP) и Microsoft Silverlight.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4dbd4-1112">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
